013|2. Support various CSV file formats and conversion options.
014|3. Enable data filtering, sorting, and aggregation functionalities.
015|

017|- As a user, I want to convert CSV files to JSON format so that I can use them in web applications.
018|- As a data analyst, I want to filter CSV data based on specific criteria so that I can focus on relevant information.
019|- As a developer, I want to aggregate data from multiple CSV files so that I can generate comprehensive reports.
020|
021|### Competitive Analysis
022|1. **Pandas**
023|   - Pros: Powerful data manipulation capabilities, widely used in data science.
024|   - Cons: Requires learning curve for new users.
025|2. **csvkit**
026|   - Pros: Command-line tools specifically for CSV files, easy to use.
027|   - Cons: Limited to CSV format only.
028|3. **OpenRefine**
029|   - Pros: Great for cleaning messy data, user-friendly interface.
030|   - Cons: Not a command-line tool, requires Java.
031|4. **Microsoft Excel**
032|   - Pros: Familiar interface for many users, powerful data analysis tools.
033|   - Cons: Not a command-line tool, can be expensive.
034|5. **Google Sheets**
035|   - Pros: Accessible from anywhere, collaborative features.
036|   - Cons: Limited functionality compared to dedicated tools.

001|# Product Requirement Document for CSV Toolkit

003|## Language & Project Info

005|- **Project Name**: csv_toolkit

008|
009|## Product Definition

011|### Product Goals
012|1. Provide a user-friendly command-line interface for CSV file manipulation.
013|2. Support various CSV file formats and conversion options.
014|3. Enable data filtering, sorting, and aggregation functionalities.
015|
016|### User Stories
017|- As a user, I want to convert CSV files to JSON format so that I can use them in web applications.
018|- As a data analyst, I want to filter CSV data based on specific criteria so that I can focus on relevant information.
019|- As a developer, I want to aggregate data from multiple CSV files so that I can generate comprehensive reports.
020|

024|   - Cons: Requires learning curve for new users.
025|2. **csvkit**
026|   - Pros: Command-line tools specifically for CSV files, easy to use.
027|   - Cons: Limited to CSV format only.
028|3. **OpenRefine**
029|   - Pros: Great for cleaning messy data, user-friendly interface.
030|   - Cons: Not a command-line tool, requires Java.
031|4. **Microsoft Excel**
032|   - Pros: Familiar interface for many users, powerful data analysis tools.
033|   - Cons: Not a command-line tool, can be expensive.
034|5. **Google Sheets**
035|   - Pros: Accessible from anywhere, collaborative features.
036|

038|
039|### Requirements Analysis

043|
044|### Requirements Pool
